     7	export const dynamic = 'force-dynamic';
     8	
     9	/**
    10	 * Login endpoint - handles user authentication
    11	 * This endpoint is rate-limited by middleware (5 requests per 2 minutes)
    12	 * Returns user data which the client uses to trigger NextAuth session creation
    13	 */
    14	export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
    15	  // Extract client info for activity logging
    16	  const { ipAddress, userAgent } = getClientInfo(req);
    17	
    18	  try {
    19	    const body = await req.json();
    20	    const { email, password } = body;
    21	
    22	    // Validate input
    23	    if (!email || !password) {
    24	      return NextResponse.json(
    25	        { error: 'ایمیل و رمز عبور الزامی است' },
    26	        { status: 400 }
    27	      );
    28	    }
    29	
    30	    // Authenticate user (throws error if invalid)
    31	    const user = await authenticateUser(email, password);
    32	
    33	    log.info('User authenticated successfully', {
    34	      userId: user.id,
    35	      email: user.email,
    36	    });
    37	
    38	    // Log successful login (fire-and-forget)
    39	    logUserActivity({
    40	      userId: user.id,
    41	      activityType: 'LOGIN_SUCCESS',
    42	      ipAddress,
    43	      userAgent,
    44	      success: true,
    45	      metadata: {
    46	        identifier_type: email.includes('@') ? 'email' : 'phone',
    47	      },
    48	    }).catch((err) => {
    49	      log.warn('Failed to log login success', {
    50	        userId: user.id,
    51	        error: err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Unknown error',
    52	      });
    53	    });
    54	
    55	    // Return user data and credentials for NextAuth signIn
    56	    return NextResponse.json({
    57	      success: true,
    58	      user: {
    59	        id: user.id,
    60	        email: user.email,
    61	        name: user.name,
    62	        role: user.role,
    63	      },
    64	    });
    65	  } catch (error) {
    66	    // Log failed login (fire-and-forget)
    67	    logUserActivity({
    68	      activityType: 'LOGIN_FAILED',
    69	      ipAddress,
    70	      userAgent,
    71	      success: false,
    72	      errorMessage: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Login failed',
    73	    }).catch((err) => {
    74	      log.warn('Failed to log login failure', {
    75	        error: err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Unknown error',
    76	      });
    77	    });
    78	
    79	    // Handle authentication errors
    80	    if (error instanceof Error) {
    81	      log.warn('Login failed', { error: error.message });
    82	      return NextResponse.json({ error: error.message }, { status: 401 });
    83	    }
    84	
    85	    log.error('Unexpected login error', { error });
    86	    return NextResponse.json(
    87	      { error: 'خطا در ورود. لطفاً دوباره تلاش کنید.' },
    88	      { status: 500 }
    89	    );
    90	  }
    91	}
     1	import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server';
     2	import { createUser, detectIdentifierType } from '@/services/user-service';
     3	import { logUserActivity } from '@/services/activity-log-service';
     4	import { getClientInfo } from '@/lib/request-utils';
     5	import { withLogging } from '@/lib/api/with-logging';
     6	import { log } from '@/lib/logger';
     7	
     8	export const dynamic = 'force-dynamic';
     9	
    10	async function postHandler(req: NextRequest) {
    11	  // Extract client info for activity logging
    12	  const { ipAddress, userAgent } = getClientInfo(req);
    13	
    14	  try {
    15	    const body = await req.json();
    16	    const { identifier, email, phone, password, name } = body;
    17	    const providedIdentifier = identifier || email || phone;
    18	
    19	    // Validate required fields (name is optional)
    20	    if (!providedIdentifier || !password) {
    21	      return NextResponse.json(
    22	        { error: 'ایمیل یا شماره تلفن به همراه رمز عبور الزامی هستند' },
    23	        { status: 400 }
    24	      );
    25	    }
    26	
    27	    const normalizedIdentifier = String(providedIdentifier).trim();
    28	    const identifierType = detectIdentifierType(normalizedIdentifier);
    29	
    30	    if (identifierType === 'invalid') {
    31	      return NextResponse.json(
    32	        { error: 'فرمت ایمیل یا شماره تلفن نامعتبر است' },
    33	        { status: 400 }
    34	      );
    35	    }
    36	
    37	    // Create user (validation happens in service)
    38	    // If name is not provided, use empty string as default
    39	    const user = await createUser({
    40	      email: identifierType === 'email' ? normalizedIdentifier : undefined,
    41	      phone: identifierType === 'phone' ? normalizedIdentifier : undefined,
    42	      password,
    43	      name: name || '',
    44	    });
    45	
    46	    // Log successful registration (fire-and-forget)
    47	    logUserActivity({
    48	      userId: user.id,
    49	      activityType: 'REGISTER',
    50	      ipAddress,
    51	      userAgent,
    52	      success: true,
    53	      metadata: {
    54	        identifier_type: identifierType,
    55	      },
    56	    }).catch((err) => {
    57	      log.warn('Failed to log registration', {
    58	        userId: user.id,
    59	        error: err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Unknown error',
    60	      });
    61	    });
    62	
    63	    return NextResponse.json(
    64	      {
    65	        success: true,
    66	        message: 'ثبت‌نام با موفقیت انجام شد',
    67	        user: {
    68	          id: user.id,
    69	          email: user.email,
    70	          name: user.name,
    71	          role: user.role,
    72	        },
    73	      },
    74	      { status: 201 }
    75	    );
    76	  } catch (error) {
    77	    console.error('Registration error:', error);
    78	
    79	    // Log failed registration (fire-and-forget)
    80	    logUserActivity({
    81	      activityType: 'REGISTER',
    82	      ipAddress,
    83	      userAgent,
    84	      success: false,
    85	      errorMessage:
    86	        error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Registration failed',
    87	    }).catch((err) => {
    88	      log.warn('Failed to log registration failure', {
    89	        error: err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Unknown error',
    90	      });
    91	    });
    92	
    93	    // Return user-friendly error message
    94	    return NextResponse.json(
    95	      { error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'خطا در ثبت‌نام' },
    96	      { status: 400 }
    97	    );
    98	  }
    99	}
   100	
   101	// Rate limiting is handled by middleware (strictLimiter, 5 req/2min)
   102	export const POST = withLogging(postHandler, 'POST /api/auth/register');

     1	/**
     2	 * SEO Configuration
     3	 * Central configuration for SEO-related constants and utilities
     4	 */
     5	import { siteConfig, siteLocale } from '@/config/site';
     6	
     7	/**
     8	 * Get the base URL for the application
     9	 * Uses environment variables with fallback to production URL
    10	 */
    11	export function getBaseUrl(): string {
    12	  // Check if we're on the server side
    13	  if (typeof window === 'undefined') {
    14	    // Server-side: use environment variable or production URL
    15	
    16	    // Priority 1: Use NEXT_PUBLIC_SITE_URL if set (allows dynamic configuration in Vercel)
    17	    const siteUrl = process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SITE_URL;
    18	    if (siteUrl) {
    19	      return siteUrl;
    20	    }
    21	
    22	    // Priority 2: Use NEXT_PUBLIC_APP_URL when configured.
    23	    const appUrl = process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_APP_URL;
    24	    if (
    25	      appUrl &&
    26	      (process.env.VERCEL_ENV !== 'production' || !appUrl.includes('localhost'))
    27	    ) {
    28	      return appUrl;
    29	    }
    30	
    31	    // Priority 3: Use VERCEL_URL for preview or production deployments.
    32	    const vercelUrl = process.env.VERCEL_URL;
    33	    if (vercelUrl && !vercelUrl.includes('localhost')) {
    34	      return `https://${vercelUrl}`;
    35	    }
    36	
    37	    // Fallback for local development.
    38	    return 'http://localhost:3000';
    39	  }
    40	
    41	  // Client-side: use window.location.origin
    42	  return window.location.origin;
    43	}
    44	
    45	/**
    46	 * Construct absolute URL from path
    47	 * @param path - Relative or absolute path
    48	 * @returns Absolute URL
    49	 */
    50	export function getAbsoluteUrl(path: string): string {
    51	  const baseUrl = getBaseUrl();
    52	
    53	  // If path is already absolute, return it
    54	  if (path.startsWith('http://') || path.startsWith('https://')) {
    55	    return path;
    56	  }
    57	
    58	  // Remove leading slash if present to avoid double slashes
    59	  const cleanPath = path.startsWith('/') ? path : `/${path}`;
    60	
    61	  return `${baseUrl}${cleanPath}`;
    62	}
    63

    65	 * Site metadata constants
    66	 */
    67	export const SITE_CONFIG = {
    68	  name: siteConfig.name,
    69	  locale: siteLocale.ogLocale,
    70	  defaultTitle: siteConfig.name,
    71	  defaultDescription: siteConfig.description,
    72	} as const;

codex
The patch adds a new configurable site URL path but leaves site-wide/product JSON-LD on the old base URL path, causing incorrect structured data for deployments using the new setting.

Review comment:

- [P2] Honor NEXT_PUBLIC_SITE_URL in JSON-LD — /data/dexter/Desktop/supabase-vercel-stack/src/lib/seo/config.ts:17-17
  With deployments that set the new `NEXT_PUBLIC_SITE_URL` but not `NEXT_PUBLIC_APP_URL`, only canonical URLs use this value; the JSON-LD helpers in `src/lib/seo/structured-data.ts` still use a private `getBaseUrl()` that ignores `NEXT_PUBLIC_SITE_URL` and falls back to `https://kitia.ir`. Since `RootLayout` emits those schemas on every page, neutral deployments will publish structured data for the old domain; please reuse this shared helper there as well.
The patch adds a new configurable site URL path but leaves site-wide/product JSON-LD on the old base URL path, causing incorrect structured data for deployments using the new setting.

  With deployments that set the new `NEXT_PUBLIC_SITE_URL` but not `NEXT_PUBLIC_APP_URL`, only canonical URLs use this value; the JSON-LD helpers in `src/lib/seo/structured-data.ts` still use a private `getBaseUrl()` that ignores `NEXT_PUBLIC_SITE_URL` and falls back to `https://kitia.ir`.
